URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS129945368	2012-08-31 14:18:37	6547	species	Common Loon	Gavia immer			4				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Washoe	US-NV-031	US-NV_974	9			Pyramid Lake--The Tamaracks	L628974	H	39.9135250	-119.5411817	2003-03-19		obsr16674	S9098535	Incidental	P20	EBIRD				3	0	G344940	0	1	0		Lin Zhu, my dad, and I went up to Pyramid Lake for half a day.  We spent--the morning at the Tamaracks and my dad went fishing while I did some--birding.  Good news is the YELLOW-BILLED LOON may still be around.  I--first noticed a largish loon straight across from the willows, fairly far--out on the lake.  Its head was brownish and the rest of its body was--darker. When the bird angled its head to the West, its bill caught the--light and it was BRIGHT YELLOW.  However, sometimes it would turn its head--the other way and the bill seemed to either be dark or not visible at--all.  This thoroughly confused me, although Lin looked at the bird once--and also caught a glimpse of the pale bill.  I watched this bird for half--an hour initially, lost it again, and then refound it as we were about to--leave.  Unfortunately, it was not any closer, but I still had the same--initial impressions.  So, if anyone goes out to Pyramid Lake in the next--couple of days, keep an eye out for it.----Also in the area:--3-4 COMMON LOONS--Most were already in or near full breeding plumage.  I saw one catch a--fish, and my dad was very jealous.--1 Horned Grebe--Western Grebes--Clark's Grebes--5 Redheads--Horned Lark--3 Killdeer--1 Song Sparrow (singing)--4 White Pelicans--Cormorants
